     │ WEEK 1-3: CITATION STRENGTH ALGORITHM                                                                                                     │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ Critical Component - Competitive with KeyCite                                                                                             │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ Tasks:                                                                                                                                    │
     │ 1. Data Collection for Training                                                                                                           │
     │   - Scrape 50,000 cases with citation networks                                                                                            │
     │   - Extract citing/cited relationships                                                                                                    │
     │   - Label treatment types (followed, distinguished, overruled)                                                                            │
     │   - Create training dataset                                                                                                               │
     │ 2. Feature Engineering                                                                                                                    │
     │ # Citation strength features                                                                                                              │
     │ features = {                                                                                                                              │
     │     'citation_count': int,           # How many times cited                                                                               │
     │     'citation_recency': float,       # Age of citing cases                                                                                │
     │     'court_authority_avg': float,    # Avg authority of citing courts                                                                     │
     │     'positive_treatment_ratio': float, # % positive treatments                                                                            │
     │     'citation_velocity': float,      # Citations per year trend                                                                           │
     │     'co-citation_centrality': float, # Network centrality score                                                                           │
     │     'citing_case_authority': list,   # Authority of each citing case                                                                      │
     │     'treatment_distribution': dict    # Distribution of treatments                                                                        │
     │ }                                                                                                                                         │
     │ 3. Algorithm Implementation                                                                                                               │
     │ # src/analytics/citation_strength.py                                                                                                      │
     │ class CitationStrengthCalculator:                                                                                                         │
     │     def calculate_strength(self, case_id):                                                                                                │
     │         # Get citation network                                                                                                            │
     │         citing_cases = self.get_citing_cases(case_id)                                                                                     │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │         # Feature calculation                                                                                                             │
     │         frequency_score = self.calc_frequency(citing_cases)                                                                               │
     │         recency_score = self.calc_recency(citing_cases)                                                                                   │
     │         authority_score = self.calc_authority(citing_cases)                                                                               │
     │         treatment_score = self.calc_treatment(citing_cases)                                                                               │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │         # Weighted combination                                                                                                            │
     │         strength = (                                                                                                                      │
     │             frequency_score * 0.30 +                                                                                                      │
     │             recency_score * 0.20 +                                                                                                        │
     │             authority_score * 0.30 +                                                                                                      │
     │             treatment_score * 0.20                                                                                                        │
     │         )                                                                                                                                 │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │         return strength  # 0-1 scale                                                                                                      │
     │ 4. Treatment Classification Model                                                                                                         │
     │   - Train classifier (BERT-based) on labeled data                                                                                         │
     │   - Classify treatments: FOLLOWED, DISTINGUISHED, OVERRULED, etc.                                                                         │
     │   - Accuracy target: >90%                                                                                                                 │
     │ 5. Integration with Neo4j                                                                                                                 │
     │   - Store citation strength scores on relationships                                                                                       │
     │   - Update scores incrementally as new cases added                                                                                        │
     │   - Create citation strength index                                                                                                        │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ Deliverables:                                                                                                                             │
     │ ✅ Citation strength algorithm implemented                                                                                                │
     │ ✅ Treatment classifier trained (>90% accuracy)                                                                                           │
     │ ✅ 50,000 cases processed with citation scores                                                                                            │
     │ ✅ Neo4j integration complete                                                                                                             │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ WEEK 4-6: QUERY UNDERSTANDING LAYER                                                                                                       │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ Tasks:                                                                                                                                    │
     │ 1. Legal Term Disambiguation                                                                                                              │
     │ # src/search/query_understanding.py                                                                                                       │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ DISAMBIGUATION_RULES = {                                                                                                                  │
     │     'partition': {                                                                                                                        │
     │         'property_law': ['property', 'estate', 'land', 'real estate'],                                                                    │
     │         'political': ['state', 'country', 'territory', 'independence']                                                                    │
     │     },                                                                                                                                    │
     │     'relief': {                                                                                                                           │
     │         'legal_remedy': ['damages', 'injunction', 'specific performance'],                                                                │
     │         'welfare': ['assistance', 'benefits', 'aid']                                                                                      │
     │     }                                                                                                                                     │
     │ }                                                                                                                                         │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ def disambiguate_term(term, query_context):                                                                                               │
     │     if term in DISAMBIGUATION_RULES:                                                                                                      │
     │         # Score each sense based on context words                                                                                         │
     │         scores = {}                                                                                                                       │
     │         for sense, keywords in DISAMBIGUATION_RULES[term].items():                                                                        │
     │             score = sum(1 for kw in keywords if kw in query_context)                                                                      │
     │             scores[sense] = score                                                                                                         │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │         return max(scores, key=scores.get)                                                                                                │
     │     return term                                                                                                                           │
     │ 2. Jurisdiction Detection                                                                                                                 │
     │   - Extract jurisdiction from query                                                                                                       │
     │   - Default to user's saved jurisdiction                                                                                                  │
     │   - Support multi-jurisdiction queries                                                                                                    │
     │ 3. Practice Area Classification                                                                                                           │
     │ # Train classifier on query → practice area                                                                                               │
     │ PRACTICE_AREAS = [                                                                                                                        │
     │     'civil', 'criminal', 'corporate', 'tax', 'family',                                                                                    │
     │     'ip', 'employment', 'real_estate', 'constitutional'                                                                                   │
     │ ]                                                                                                                                         │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ practice_area = classifier.predict(query)                                                                                                 │
     │ # Use to filter/boost relevant documents                                                                                                  │
     │ 4. Intent Classification                                                                                                                  │
     │ INTENT_TYPES = [                                                                                                                          │
     │     'research',        # "What is the law on X?"                                                                                          │
     │     'cite_check',      # "Validate citation for X"                                                                                        │
     │     'case_find',       # "Find similar cases"                                                                                             │
     │     'statute_lookup',  # "Section 302 IPC"                                                                                                │
     │     'update_check'     # "Has X been overruled?"                                                                                          │
     │ ]                                                                                                                                         │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ intent = intent_classifier.predict(query)                                                                                                 │
     │ # Customize retrieval strategy based on intent                                                                                            │
     │ 5. Temporal Query Parsing                                                                                                                 │
     │   - Extract date constraints ("recent", "2020-2023", "since 2015")                                                                        │
     │   - Convert to effective date filters                                                                                                     │
     │   - Support "law as of date" queries                                                                                                      │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ Deliverables:                                                                                                                             │
     │ ✅ Query understanding pipeline operational                                                                                               │
     │ ✅ Disambiguation accuracy >85%                                                                                                           │
     │ ✅ Intent classification accuracy >90%                                                                                                    │
     │ ✅ Temporal parsing working                                                                                                               │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ WEEK 7-9: NAMED ENTITY RECOGNITION                                                                                                        │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ Technology: Legal-BERT + Custom Training                                                                                                  │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ Tasks:                                                                                                                                    │
     │ 1. Data Labeling                                                                                                                          │
     │   - Label 5,000 legal documents for entities                                                                                              │
     │   - Entity types: Judge, Attorney, Firm, Statute, Section, Doctrine, Cause_of_Action                                                      │
     │   - Use Label Studio for annotation                                                                                                       │
     │ 2. Model Training                                                                                                                         │
     │ # Fine-tune Legal-BERT for NER                                                                                                            │
     │ from transformers import AutoModelForTokenClassification, Trainer                                                                         │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ model = AutoModelForTokenClassification.from_pretrained(                                                                                  │
     │     "nlpaueb/legal-bert-base-uncased",                                                                                                    │
     │     num_labels=len(ENTITY_TYPES)                                                                                                          │
     │ )                                                                                                                                         │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ trainer = Trainer(                                                                                                                        │
     │     model=model,                                                                                                                          │
     │     train_dataset=train_dataset,                                                                                                          │
     │     eval_dataset=eval_dataset,                                                                                                            │
     │     compute_metrics=compute_ner_metrics                                                                                                   │
     │ )                                                                                                                                         │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ trainer.train()                                                                                                                           │
     │ # Target: F1 score >92%                                                                                                                   │
     │ 3. Citation Extraction (Regex + NER)                                                                                                      │
     │ # Regex patterns for case citations                                                                                                       │
     │ CASE_CITATION_PATTERNS = [                                                                                                                │
     │     r'\d+\s+[A-Z]+\s+\d+',           # "123 SCC 456"                                                                                      │
     │     r'\d+\s+DLR\s+\(\d{4}\)\s+\d+',  # "67 DLR (2015) 534"                                                                                │
     │     r'\[\d{4}\]\s+\d+\s+[A-Z]+'      # "[2015] 1 SCR 123"                                                                                 │
     │ ]                                                                                                                                         │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ # Statute section patterns                                                                                                                │
     │ STATUTE_PATTERNS = [                                                                                                                      │
     │     r'Section\s+\d+[A-Z]*',          # "Section 302"                                                                                      │
     │     r'Article\s+\d+',                # "Article 21"                                                                                       │
     │     r'§\s*\d+'                       # "§ 1983"                                                                                           │
     │ ]                                                                                                                                         │
     │ 4. Entity Linking                                                                                                                         │
     │   - Link extracted entities to knowledge graph                                                                                            │
     │   - Disambiguate entity mentions                                                                                                          │
     │   - Create entity index                                                                                                                   │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ Deliverables:                                                                                                                             │
     │ ✅ NER model trained (F1 >92%)                                                                                                            │
     │ ✅ Citation extraction operational                                                                                                        │
     │ ✅ Entity linking to Neo4j working                                                                                                        │
     │ ✅ 5,000 documents processed with entities                                                                                                │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ WEEK 10-12: CROSS-ENCODER RERANKING                                                                                                       │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ Technology: Cohere Rerank v3 (API) initially, migrate to self-hosted later                                                                │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ Tasks:                                                                                                                                    │
     │ 1. Reranking Integration                                                                                                                  │
     │ # src/search/reranker.py                                                                                                                  │
     │ import cohere                                                                                                                             │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ co = cohere.Client(api_key=COHERE_API_KEY)                                                                                                │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ def rerank(query, documents, top_k=20):                                                                                                   │
     │     # Prepare documents for reranking                                                                                                     │
     │     docs_for_rerank = [doc['chunk_text'] for doc in documents]                                                                            │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │     # Call Cohere Rerank API                                                                                                              │
     │     results = co.rerank(                                                                                                                  │
     │         query=query,                                                                                                                      │
     │         documents=docs_for_rerank,                                                                                                        │
     │         top_n=top_k,                                                                                                                      │
     │         model='rerank-english-v3.0'                                                                                                       │
     │     )                                                                                                                                     │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │     # Reorder original documents based on reranking                                                                                       │
     │     reranked_docs = [documents[r.index] for r in results.results]                                                                         │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │     return reranked_docs                                                                                                                  │
     │ 2. Cost Optimization Strategy                                                                                                             │
     │   - Phase 1: Use Cohere API (fast deployment)                                                                                             │
     │   - Phase 2: Train custom reranker on collected data                                                                                      │
     │   - Phase 3: Self-host custom reranker (save $20K/year)                                                                                   │
     │ 3. Evaluation Dataset                                                                                                                     │
     │   - Create 1,000 query-document pairs                                                                                                     │
     │   - Expert lawyers label relevance (1-5 scale)                                                                                            │
     │   - Use for reranker evaluation                                                                                                           │
     │   - Track NDCG@10 improvement                                                                                                             │
     │ 4. A/B Testing Setup                                                                                                                      │
     │   - Control: No reranking                                                                                                                 │
     │   - Treatment: With reranking                                                                                                             │
     │   - Measure: Precision@10, user click-through rate                                                                                        │
     │   - Target: +15% improvement                                                                                                              │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ Deliverables:                                                                                                                             │
     │ ✅ Cohere Rerank integrated                                                                                                               │
     │ ✅ Reranking evaluation dataset (1,000 pairs)                                                                                             │
     │ ✅ A/B testing framework operational                                                                                                      │

     │ WEEK 1-2: Data Pipeline Architecture                                                                                                      │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ 1. Source Integration                                                                                                                     │
     │ # src/ingestion/sources/                                                                                                                  │
     │ - indiankanoon_scraper.py                                                                                                                 │
     │ - bdlaws_scraper.py                                                                                                                       │
     │ - uk_bailii_scraper.py                                                                                                                    │
     │ - scottish_courts_scraper.py                                                                                                              │
     │ - eu_eur_lex_scraper.py                                                                                                                   │
     │ 2. ETL Pipeline (Apache Airflow)                                                                                                          │
     │ # dags/legal_document_ingestion.py                                                                                                        │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ @dag(schedule_interval='@daily')                                                                                                          │
     │ def legal_document_ingestion():                                                                                                           │
     │     # Task 1: Scrape new documents                                                                                                        │
     │     scrape_task = PythonOperator(                                                                                                         │
     │         task_id='scrape_documents',                                                                                                       │
     │         python_callable=scrape_all_sources                                                                                                │
     │     )                                                                                                                                     │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │     # Task 2: OCR processing (if needed)                                                                                                  │
     │     ocr_task = PythonOperator(                                                                                                            │
     │         task_id='ocr_processing',                                                                                                         │
     │         python_callable=process_pdfs                                                                                                      │
     │     )                                                                                                                                     │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │     # Task 3: Metadata extraction                                                                                                         │
     │     metadata_task = PythonOperator(                                                                                                       │
     │         task_id='extract_metadata',                                                                                                       │
     │         python_callable=extract_metadata                                                                                                  │
     │     )                                                                                                                                     │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │     # Task 4: Chunking                                                                                                                    │
     │     chunk_task = PythonOperator(                                                                                                          │
     │         task_id='chunk_documents',                                                                                                        │
     │         python_callable=chunk_documents                                                                                                   │
     │     )                                                                                                                                     │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │     # Task 5: Generate embeddings                                                                                                         │
     │     embed_task = PythonOperator(                                                                                                          │
     │         task_id='generate_embeddings',                                                                                                    │
     │         python_callable=generate_embeddings                                                                                               │
     │     )                                                                                                                                     │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │     # Task 6: Index to Weaviate + Neo4j                                                                                                   │
     │     index_task = PythonOperator(                                                                                                          │
     │         task_id='index_documents',                                                                                                        │
     │         python_callable=index_to_databases                                                                                                │
     │     )                                                                                                                                     │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │     scrape_task >> ocr_task >> metadata_task >> chunk_task >> embed_task >> index_task                                                    │
     │ 3. Data Quality Checks                                                                                                                    │
     │   - Validate required fields present                                                                                                      │
     │   - Check text extraction quality                                                                                                         │
     │   - Verify citation extraction                                                                                                            │

     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ WEEK 3-6: Intelligent Chunking Implementation                                                                                             │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ # src/chunking/intelligent_chunker.py                                                                                                     │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ class IntelligentLegalChunker:                                                                                                            │
     │     """                                                                                                                                   │
     │     Document type-aware chunking with 65 chunk types                                                                                      │
     │     """                                                                                                                                   │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │     def chunk_document(self, document):                                                                                                   │
     │         doc_type = document['document_type']                                                                                              │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │         if doc_type in ['judgment', 'opinion', 'decision']:                                                                               │
     │             return self.chunk_judgment(document)                                                                                          │
     │         elif doc_type in ['statute', 'act', 'code']:                                                                                      │
     │             return self.chunk_statute(document)                                                                                           │
     │         elif doc_type in ['contract', 'agreement']:                                                                                       │
     │             return self.chunk_contract(document)                                                                                          │
     │         else:                                                                                                                             │
     │             return self.chunk_generic(document)                                                                                           │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │     def chunk_judgment(self, doc):                                                                                                        │
     │         """                                                                                                                               │
     │         Semantic chunking for judgments                                                                                                   │
     │         Size: 600-800 tokens, 150 token overlap                                                                                           │
     │         """                                                                                                                               │
     │         # Extract sections using LLM                                                                                                      │
     │         sections = self.extract_judgment_sections(doc)                                                                                    │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │         chunks = []                                                                                                                       │
     │         for section in sections:                                                                                                          │
     │             section_type = self.classify_section(section)  # facts, holding, reasoning, etc.                                              │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │             # Chunk large sections                                                                                                        │
     │             if len(section.split()) > 800:                                                                                                │
     │                 sub_chunks = self.semantic_split(section, max_tokens=800, overlap=150)                                                    │
     │                 for sub_chunk in sub_chunks:                                                                                              │
     │                     chunks.append({                                                                                                       │
     │                         'chunk_text': self.prepend_metadata(doc, sub_chunk),                                                              │
     │                         'chunk_type': section_type,                                                                                       │
     │                         'token_count': len(sub_chunk.split()),                                                                            │
     │                         'start_char': sub_chunk_start,                                                                                    │
     │                         'end_char': sub_chunk_end                                                                                         │
     │                     })                                                                                                                    │
     │             else:                                                                                                                         │
     │                 chunks.append({                                                                                                           │
     │                     'chunk_text': self.prepend_metadata(doc, section),                                                                    │
     │                     'chunk_type': section_type,                                                                                           │
     │                     'token_count': len(section.split()),                                                                                  │
     │                     'start_char': section_start,                                                                                          │
     │                     'end_char': section_end                                                                                               │
     │                 })                                                                                                                        │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │         return chunks                                                                                                                     │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │     def chunk_statute(self, doc):                                                                                                         │
     │         """                                                                                                                               │
     │         Hierarchical chunking for statutes                                                                                                │
     │         Size: Section-based (200-600 tokens), no overlap                                                                                  │
     │         """                                                                                                                               │
     │         sections = self.extract_statute_sections(doc)                                                                                     │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │         chunks = []                                                                                                                       │
     │         for section in sections:                                                                                                          │
     │             chunk_text = self.format_statute_chunk(doc, section)                                                                          │
     │             chunk_type = self.classify_statute_chunk(section)  # section, subsection, definition, etc.                                    │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │             chunks.append({                                                                                                               │
     │                 'chunk_text': chunk_text,                                                                                                 │
     │                 'chunk_type': chunk_type,                                                                                                 │
     │                 'section_number': section['number'],                                                                                      │
     │                 'token_count': len(chunk_text.split())                                                                                    │
     │             })                                                                                                                            │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │         return chunks                                                                                                                     │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │     def prepend_metadata(self, doc, chunk_text):                                                                                          │
     │         """                                                                                                                               │
     │         Prepend document metadata to improve retrieval                                                                                    │
     │         Format:                                                                                                                           │
     │         Case: [Title]                                                                                                                     │
     │         Court: [Court Name]                                                                                                               │
     │         Date: [Date]                                                                                                                      │
     │         Citation: [Citation]                                                                                                              │
     │         Type: [Chunk Type]                                                                                                                │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │         [chunk_text]                                                                                                                      │
     │         """                                                                                                                               │
     │         metadata = f"""Case: {doc['title']}                                                                                               │
     │ Court: {doc['court']}                                                                                                                     │
     │ Date: {doc['date']}                                                                                                                       │
     │ Citation: {doc['citation']}                                                                                                               │
     │ Jurisdiction: {doc['jurisdiction']}                                                                                                       │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ {chunk_text}"""                                                                                                                           │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │         return metadata                                                                                                                   │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
