     │ PHASE 1B: ANALYTICS DEVELOPMENT (Months 7-10, Parallel to 1A) - $300K | 3 FTE                                                             │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ OBJECTIVE: Judge/attorney analytics, outcome prediction                                                                                   │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ TEAM COMPOSITION                                                                                                                          │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ - Senior Data Scientist (full-time) - ML models                                                                                           │
     │ - Backend Engineer (full-time) - Analytics API                                                                                            │
     │ - Frontend Engineer (part-time) - Dashboard UI                                                                                            │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ WEEK 1-4: Judge Analytics                                                                                                                 │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ Data Collection:                                                                                                                          │
     │ -- Aggregate judge statistics                                                                                                             │
     │ WITH judge_cases AS (                                                                                                                     │
     │     SELECT                                                                                                                                │
     │         j.judge_id,                                                                                                                       │
     │         j.name,                                                                                                                           │
     │         c.case_id,                                                                                                                        │
     │         c.decision_date,                                                                                                                  │
     │         c.disposition,                                                                                                                    │
     │         c.case_type,                                                                                                                      │
     │         c.plaintiff_attorney,                                                                                                             │
     │         c.defendant_attorney                                                                                                              │
     │     FROM judges j                                                                                                                         │
     │     JOIN case_judges cj ON j.judge_id = cj.judge_id                                                                                       │
     │     JOIN cases c ON cj.case_id = c.case_id                                                                                                │
     │ )                                                                                                                                         │
     │ SELECT                                                                                                                                    │
     │     judge_id,                                                                                                                             │
     │     name,                                                                                                                                 │
     │     COUNT(*) as total_cases,                                                                                                              │
     │     AVG(CASE WHEN disposition = 'plaintiff_win' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as plaintiff_win_rate,                                                 │
     │     COUNT(*) FILTER (WHERE case_type = 'motion_to_dismiss') as mtd_cases,                                                                 │
     │     AVG(CASE WHEN case_type = 'motion_to_dismiss' AND disposition = 'granted' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as mtd_grant_rate                        │
     │ FROM judge_cases                                                                                                                          │
     │ GROUP BY judge_id, name;                                                                                                                  │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ Analytics Calculations:                                                                                                                   │
     │ # src/analytics/judge_analytics.py                                                                                                        │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ class JudgeAnalytics:                                                                                                                     │
     │     def calculate_metrics(self, judge_id):                                                                                                │
     │         cases = self.get_judge_cases(judge_id)                                                                                            │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │         return {                                                                                                                          │
     │             'total_cases': len(cases),                                                                                                    │
     │             'win_rates': {                                                                                                                │
     │                 'plaintiff': self.calc_win_rate(cases, 'plaintiff'),                                                                      │
     │                 'defendant': self.calc_win_rate(cases, 'defendant')                                                                       │
     │             },                                                                                                                            │
     │             'motion_grant_rates': {                                                                                                       │
     │                 'motion_to_dismiss': self.calc_motion_rate(cases, 'motion_to_dismiss'),                                                   │
     │                 'summary_judgment': self.calc_motion_rate(cases, 'summary_judgment')                                                      │
     │             },                                                                                                                            │
     │             'reversal_rate': self.calc_reversal_rate(judge_id),                                                                           │
     │             'average_duration': self.calc_avg_duration(cases),                                                                            │
     │             'settlement_rate': self.calc_settlement_rate(cases),                                                                          │
     │             'specializations': self.identify_specializations(cases),                                                                      │
     │             'reputation_score': self.calc_reputation_score(judge_id)                                                                      │
     │         }                                                                                                                                 │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ Deliverables:                                                                                                                             │
     │ ✅ Judge analytics calculated for all judges                                                                                              │
     │ ✅ Analytics API endpoints operational                                                                                                    │
     │ ✅ Dashboard showing judge statistics                                                                                                     │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ WEEK 5-8: Case Outcome Prediction Model                                                                                                   │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ Model Development:                                                                                                                        │
     │ # src/ml/outcome_prediction.py                                                                                                            │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ from xgboost import XGBClassifier                                                                                                         │
     │ from sklearn.model_selection import train_test_split                                                                                      │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ class OutcomePredictionModel:                                                                                                             │
     │     def __init__(self):                                                                                                                   │
     │         self.model = XGBClassifier(                                                                                                       │
     │             n_estimators=100,                                                                                                             │
     │             max_depth=8,                                                                                                                  │
     │             learning_rate=0.1                                                                                                             │
     │         )                                                                                                                                 │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │     def prepare_features(self, case):                                                                                                     │
     │         return {                                                                                                                          │
     │             # Case characteristics                                                                                                        │
     │             'case_type': self.encode_case_type(case['case_type']),                                                                        │
     │             'jurisdiction': self.encode_jurisdiction(case['jurisdiction']),                                                               │
     │             'case_complexity': self.calculate_complexity(case),                                                                           │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │             # Judge features                                                                                                              │
     │             'judge_plaintiff_win_rate': self.get_judge_win_rate(case['judge_id'], 'plaintiff'),                                           │
     │             'judge_reversal_rate': self.get_judge_reversal_rate(case['judge_id']),                                                        │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │             # Attorney features                                                                                                           │
     │             'plaintiff_attorney_win_rate': self.get_attorney_win_rate(case['plaintiff_attorney']),                                        │
     │             'defendant_attorney_win_rate': self.get_attorney_win_rate(case['defendant_attorney']),                                        │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │             # Case history features                                                                                                       │
     │             'motion_history': self.encode_motion_history(case),                                                                           │
     │             'discovery_disputes': case['discovery_disputes_count'],                                                                       │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │             # Precedent features                                                                                                          │
     │             'precedent_strength': self.calculate_precedent_strength(case),                                                                │
     │             'similar_case_outcomes': self.get_similar_case_stats(case)                                                                    │
     │         }                                                                                                                                 │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │     def train(self, training_data):                                                                                                       │
     │         X = [self.prepare_features(case) for case in training_data]                                                                       │
     │         y = [case['outcome'] for case in training_data]  # 0=defendant_win, 1=plaintiff_win, 2=settlement                                 │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │         X_train, X_test, y_train, y_test = train_test_split(X, y, test_size=0.2)                                                          │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │         self.model.fit(X_train, y_train)                                                                                                  │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │         accuracy = self.model.score(X_test, y_test)                                                                                       │
     │         print(f"Model accuracy: {accuracy}")  # Target: >75%                                                                              │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │     def predict(self, case):                                                                                                              │
     │         features = self.prepare_features(case)                                                                                            │
     │         probabilities = self.model.predict_proba([features])[0]                                                                           │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │         return {                                                                                                                          │
     │             'defendant_win_probability': probabilities[0],                                                                                │
     │             'plaintiff_win_probability': probabilities[1],                                                                                │
     │             'settlement_probability': probabilities[2],                                                                                   │
     │             'confidence': max(probabilities)                                                                                              │
     │         }                                                                                                                                 │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ Model Training:                                                                                                                           │
     │ - Collect 50,000 historical cases with known outcomes                                                                                     │
     │ - Train XGBoost model                                                                                                                     │
     │ - Achieve >75% accuracy target                                                                                                            │
     │ - Deploy model behind API                                                                                                                 │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ Deliverables:                                                                                                                             │
     │ ✅ Outcome prediction model trained (>75% accuracy)                                                                                       │
     │ ✅ API endpoint for predictions                                                                                                           │
     │ ✅ Model monitoring dashboard                                                                                                             │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ WEEK 9-12: Monitoring & Alerts System                                                                                                     │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ System Architecture:                                                                                                                      │
     │ # src/alerts/alert_system.py                                                                                                              │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ class LegalAlertSystem:                                                                                                                   │
     │     def __init__(self):                                                                                                                   │
     │         self.subscribers = {}                                                                                                             │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │     def subscribe(self, user_id, alert_type, filters):                                                                                    │
     │         """                                                                                                                               │
     │         Alert types:                                                                                                                      │
     │         - new_case_law                                                                                                                    │
     │         - statute_change                                                                                                                  │
     │         - adverse_citation                                                                                                                │
     │         - court_filing                                                                                                                    │
     │         - saved_search                                                                                                                    │
     │         """                                                                                                                               │
     │         alert = {                                                                                                                         │
     │             'user_id': user_id,                                                                                                           │
     │             'alert_type': alert_type,                                                                                                     │
     │             'filters': filters,                                                                                                           │
     │             'frequency': 'daily',  # or 'weekly', 'instant'                                                                               │
     │             'delivery': ['email', 'webhook']                                                                                              │
     │         }                                                                                                                                 │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │         self.store_subscription(alert)                                                                                                    │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │     def check_new_documents(self):                                                                                                        │
     │         """                                                                                                                               │
     │         Run daily job to check for matching documents                                                                                     │
     │         """                                                                                                                               │
     │         new_docs = self.get_documents_since_last_check()                                                                                  │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │         for doc in new_docs:                                                                                                              │
     │             matching_alerts = self.find_matching_subscriptions(doc)                                                                       │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │             for alert in matching_alerts:                                                                                                 │
     │                 self.send_notification(alert, doc)                                                                                        │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │     def check_adverse_citations(self):                                                                                                    │
     │         """                                                                                                                               │
     │         Check if user's saved cases have been distinguished/overruled                                                                     │
     │         """                                                                                                                               │
     │         for user_id in self.get_active_users():                                                                                           │
     │             saved_cases = self.get_user_saved_cases(user_id)                                                                              │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │             for case in saved_cases:                                                                                                      │
     │                 new_citations = self.get_new_citations(case['case_id'])                                                                   │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │                 adverse = [c for c in new_citations if c['treatment'] in ['DISTINGUISHED', 'OVERRULED', 'QUESTIONED']]                    │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │                 if adverse:                                                                                                               │
     │                     self.send_adverse_citation_alert(user_id, case, adverse)                                                              │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ Notification Channels:                                                                                                                    │
     │ - Email (SendGrid)                                                                                                                        │
     │ - SMS (Twilio) - for urgent alerts                                                                                                        │
     │ - Webhooks (for your agentic AI system)                                                                                                   │
     │ - In-app notifications                                                                                                                    │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ Deliverables:                                                                                                                             │
     │ ✅ Alert system operational                                                                                                               │
     │ ✅ 5 alert types implemented                                                                                                              │
     │ ✅ Email/SMS/webhook delivery working                                                                                                     │
     │ ✅ User subscription management                                                                                                           │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ ---                                                                                                                                       │

     │                                                                                                                                           │

     │ SECTION 4: TECHNOLOGY STACK (FINAL DECISIONS)                                                                                             │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ | Component     | Technology                | Rationale                                |                                                  │
     │ |---------------|---------------------------|------------------------------------------|                                                  │
     │ | Cloud         | GCP                       | Best ML/AI services, competitive pricing |                                                  │
     │ | Orchestration | Kubernetes (GKE)          | Scalability, portability                 |                                                  │
     │ | Vector DB     | Weaviate Cloud            | Managed, hybrid search, cost-effective   |                                                  │
     │ | Graph DB      | Neo4j Aura Enterprise     | Managed, ACID, Cypher query language     |                                                  │
     │ | Search        | Elasticsearch 8.x         | BM25, full-text search                   |                                                  │
     │ | Embeddings    | BGE-M3 (self-hosted)      | 1024-dim, multilingual, open-source      |                                                  │
     │ | Reranker      | Cohere Rerank v3 → Custom | Start commercial, migrate to self-hosted |                                                  │
     │ | LLM           | GPT-4 / Gemini 2.0 Flash  | Issue tagging, headnotes, synthesis      |                                                  │
     │ | NER           | Legal-BERT fine-tuned     | Best for legal entities                  |                                                  │
     │ | API           | FastAPI (Python 3.11)     | Fast, async, OpenAPI docs                |                                                  │
     │ | ETL           | Apache Airflow            | Workflow orchestration                   |                                                  │
     │ | CI/CD         | GitHub Actions            | Native Git integration                   |                                                  │
     │ | Monitoring    | Prometheus + Grafana      | Open-source, powerful                    |                                                  │
     │ | Logging       | Loki + Promtail           | Integrates with Grafana                  |                                                  │
     │ | Database      | PostgreSQL 15             | Metadata, user data                      |                                                  │
     │ | Cache         | Redis                     | Session, query caching                   |                                                  │
     │ | Message Queue | RabbitMQ                  | Task distribution                        |                                                  │
     │                                                                                                                                           │

     │ Unit Tests (90% coverage target):                                                                                                         │
     │ # tests/test_chunking.py                                                                                                                  │
     │ def test_judgment_chunking():                                                                                                             │
     │     doc = load_test_judgment()                                                                                                            │
     │     chunks = chunker.chunk_judgment(doc)                                                                                                  │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │     assert len(chunks) > 0                                                                                                                │
     │     assert all(chunk['chunk_type'] in VALID_TYPES for chunk in chunks)                                                                    │
     │     assert all(chunk['token_count'] <= 800 for chunk in chunks)                                                                           │
     │                                                                                                                                           │

     │ - API endpoint tests                                                                                                                      │

     │ ]                                                                                                                                         │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ # Statute section patterns                                                                                                                │
     │ STATUTE_PATTERNS = [                                                                                                                      │

     │ WEEK 10-12: CROSS-ENCODER RERANKING                                                                                                       │
     │                                                                                                                                           │

     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ Tasks:                                                                                                                                    │
     │ 1. Reranking Integration                                                                                                                  │
     │ # src/search/reranker.py                                                                                                                  │
     │ import cohere                                                                                                                             │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ co = cohere.Client(api_key=COHERE_API_KEY)                                                                                                │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ def rerank(query, documents, top_k=20):                                                                                                   │
     │     # Prepare documents for reranking                                                                                                     │
     │     docs_for_rerank = [doc['chunk_text'] for doc in documents]                                                                            │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │     # Call Cohere Rerank API                                                                                                              │
     │     results = co.rerank(                                                                                                                  │
     │         query=query,                                                                                                                      │
     │         documents=docs_for_rerank,                                                                                                        │
     │         top_n=top_k,                                                                                                                      │
     │         model='rerank-english-v3.0'                                                                                                       │
     │     )                                                                                                                                     │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │     # Reorder original documents based on reranking                                                                                       │
     │     reranked_docs = [documents[r.index] for r in results.results]                                                                         │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │     return reranked_docs                                                                                                                  │

     │ def legal_document_ingestion():                                                                                                           │
     │     # Task 1: Scrape new documents                                                                                                        │
     │     scrape_task = PythonOperator(                                                                                                         │
     │         task_id='scrape_documents',                                                                                                       │
     │         python_callable=scrape_all_sources                                                                                                │
     │     )                                                                                                                                     │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │     # Task 2: OCR processing (if needed)                                                                                                  │
     │     ocr_task = PythonOperator(                                                                                                            │
     │         task_id='ocr_processing',                                                                                                         │
     │         python_callable=process_pdfs                                                                                                      │
     │     )                                                                                                                                     │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │     # Task 3: Metadata extraction                                                                                                         │
     │     metadata_task = PythonOperator(                                                                                                       │
     │         task_id='extract_metadata',                                                                                                       │
     │         python_callable=extract_metadata                                                                                                  │
     │     )                                                                                                                                     │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │     # Task 4: Chunking                                                                                                                    │
     │     chunk_task = PythonOperator(                                                                                                          │
     │         task_id='chunk_documents',                                                                                                        │
     │         python_callable=chunk_documents                                                                                                   │
     │     )                                                                                                                                     │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │     # Task 5: Generate embeddings                                                                                                         │
     │     embed_task = PythonOperator(                                                                                                          │
     │         task_id='generate_embeddings',                                                                                                    │
     │         python_callable=generate_embeddings                                                                                               │
     │     )                                                                                                                                     │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │     # Task 6: Index to Weaviate + Neo4j                                                                                                   │
     │     index_task = PythonOperator(                                                                                                          │
     │         task_id='index_documents',                                                                                                        │
     │         python_callable=index_to_databases                                                                                                │
     │     )                                                                                                                                     │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │     scrape_task >> ocr_task >> metadata_task >> chunk_task >> embed_task >> index_task                                                    │

     │ WEEK 3-6: Intelligent Chunking Implementation                                                                                             │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ # src/chunking/intelligent_chunker.py                                                                                                     │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ class IntelligentLegalChunker:                                                                                                            │
     │     """                                                                                                                                   │
     │     Document type-aware chunking with 65 chunk types                                                                                      │
     │     """                                                                                                                                   │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │     def chunk_document(self, document):                                                                                                   │
     │         doc_type = document['document_type']                                                                                              │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │         if doc_type in ['judgment', 'opinion', 'decision']:                                                                               │
     │             return self.chunk_judgment(document)                                                                                          │
     │         elif doc_type in ['statute', 'act', 'code']:                                                                                      │
     │             return self.chunk_statute(document)                                                                                           │
     │         elif doc_type in ['contract', 'agreement']:                                                                                       │
     │             return self.chunk_contract(document)                                                                                          │
     │         else:                                                                                                                             │
     │             return self.chunk_generic(document)                                                                                           │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │     def chunk_judgment(self, doc):                                                                                                        │
     │         """                                                                                                                               │
     │         Semantic chunking for judgments                                                                                                   │
     │         Size: 600-800 tokens, 150 token overlap                                                                                           │
     │         """                                                                                                                               │
     │         # Extract sections using LLM                                                                                                      │
     │         sections = self.extract_judgment_sections(doc)                                                                                    │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │         chunks = []                                                                                                                       │
     │         for section in sections:                                                                                                          │
     │             section_type = self.classify_section(section)  # facts, holding, reasoning, etc.                                              │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │             # Chunk large sections                                                                                                        │
     │             if len(section.split()) > 800:                                                                                                │
     │                 sub_chunks = self.semantic_split(section, max_tokens=800, overlap=150)                                                    │
     │                 for sub_chunk in sub_chunks:                                                                                              │
     │                     chunks.append({                                                                                                       │
     │                         'chunk_text': self.prepend_metadata(doc, sub_chunk),                                                              │
     │                         'chunk_type': section_type,                                                                                       │
     │                         'token_count': len(sub_chunk.split()),                                                                            │
     │                         'start_char': sub_chunk_start,                                                                                    │
     │                         'end_char': sub_chunk_end                                                                                         │
     │                     })                                                                                                                    │
     │             else:                                                                                                                         │
     │                 chunks.append({                                                                                                           │
     │                     'chunk_text': self.prepend_metadata(doc, section),                                                                    │
     │                     'chunk_type': section_type,                                                                                           │
     │                     'token_count': len(section.split()),                                                                                  │
     │                     'start_char': section_start,                                                                                          │
     │                     'end_char': section_end                                                                                               │
     │                 })                                                                                                                        │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │         return chunks                                                                                                                     │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │     def chunk_statute(self, doc):                                                                                                         │
     │         """                                                                                                                               │
     │         Hierarchical chunking for statutes                                                                                                │
     │         Size: Section-based (200-600 tokens), no overlap                                                                                  │
     │         """                                                                                                                               │
     │         sections = self.extract_statute_sections(doc)                                                                                     │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │         chunks = []                                                                                                                       │
     │         for section in sections:                                                                                                          │
     │             chunk_text = self.format_statute_chunk(doc, section)                                                                          │
     │             chunk_type = self.classify_statute_chunk(section)  # section, subsection, definition, etc.                                    │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │             chunks.append({                                                                                                               │
     │                 'chunk_text': chunk_text,                                                                                                 │
     │                 'chunk_type': chunk_type,                                                                                                 │
     │                 'section_number': section['number'],                                                                                      │
     │                 'token_count': len(chunk_text.split())                                                                                    │
     │             })                                                                                                                            │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │         return chunks                                                                                                                     │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │     def prepend_metadata(self, doc, chunk_text):                                                                                          │
     │         """                                                                                                                               │
     │         Prepend document metadata to improve retrieval                                                                                    │
     │         Format:                                                                                                                           │
     │         Case: [Title]                                                                                                                     │
     │         Court: [Court Name]                                                                                                               │
     │         Date: [Date]                                                                                                                      │
     │         Citation: [Citation]                                                                                                              │
     │         Type: [Chunk Type]                                                                                                                │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │         [chunk_text]                                                                                                                      │
     │         """                                                                                                                               │
     │         metadata = f"""Case: {doc['title']}                                                                                               │
     │ Court: {doc['court']}                                                                                                                     │
     │ Date: {doc['date']}                                                                                                                       │
     │ Citation: {doc['citation']}                                                                                                               │
     │ Jurisdiction: {doc['jurisdiction']}                                                                                                       │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ {chunk_text}"""                                                                                                                           │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │         return metadata                                                                                                                   │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
