     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ WEEK 1-4: Judge Analytics                                                                                                                 │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ Data Collection:                                                                                                                          │
     │ -- Aggregate judge statistics                                                                                                             │
     │ WITH judge_cases AS (                                                                                                                     │
     │     SELECT                                                                                                                                │
     │         j.judge_id,                                                                                                                       │
     │         j.name,                                                                                                                           │
     │         c.case_id,                                                                                                                        │
     │         c.decision_date,                                                                                                                  │
     │         c.disposition,                                                                                                                    │
     │         c.case_type,                                                                                                                      │
     │         c.plaintiff_attorney,                                                                                                             │
     │         c.defendant_attorney                                                                                                              │
     │     FROM judges j                                                                                                                         │
     │     JOIN case_judges cj ON j.judge_id = cj.judge_id                                                                                       │
     │     JOIN cases c ON cj.case_id = c.case_id                                                                                                │
     │ )                                                                                                                                         │
     │ SELECT                                                                                                                                    │
     │     judge_id,                                                                                                                             │
     │     name,                                                                                                                                 │
     │     COUNT(*) as total_cases,                                                                                                              │
     │     AVG(CASE WHEN disposition = 'plaintiff_win' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as plaintiff_win_rate,                                                 │
     │     COUNT(*) FILTER (WHERE case_type = 'motion_to_dismiss') as mtd_cases,                                                                 │
     │     AVG(CASE WHEN case_type = 'motion_to_dismiss' AND disposition = 'granted' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as mtd_grant_rate                        │
     │ FROM judge_cases                                                                                                                          │
     │ GROUP BY judge_id, name;                                                                                                                  │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ Analytics Calculations:                                                                                                                   │
     │ # src/analytics/judge_analytics.py                                                                                                        │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ class JudgeAnalytics:                                                                                                                     │
     │     def calculate_metrics(self, judge_id):                                                                                                │
     │         cases = self.get_judge_cases(judge_id)                                                                                            │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │         return {                                                                                                                          │
     │             'total_cases': len(cases),                                                                                                    │
     │             'win_rates': {                                                                                                                │
     │                 'plaintiff': self.calc_win_rate(cases, 'plaintiff'),                                                                      │
     │                 'defendant': self.calc_win_rate(cases, 'defendant')                                                                       │
     │             },                                                                                                                            │
     │             'motion_grant_rates': {                                                                                                       │
     │                 'motion_to_dismiss': self.calc_motion_rate(cases, 'motion_to_dismiss'),                                                   │
     │                 'summary_judgment': self.calc_motion_rate(cases, 'summary_judgment')                                                      │
     │             },                                                                                                                            │
     │             'reversal_rate': self.calc_reversal_rate(judge_id),                                                                           │
     │             'average_duration': self.calc_avg_duration(cases),                                                                            │
     │             'settlement_rate': self.calc_settlement_rate(cases),                                                                          │
     │             'specializations': self.identify_specializations(cases),                                                                      │
     │             'reputation_score': self.calc_reputation_score(judge_id)                                                                      │
     │         }                                                                                                                                 │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ Deliverables:                                                                                                                             │
     │ ✅ Judge analytics calculated for all judges                                                                                              │
     │ ✅ Analytics API endpoints operational                                                                                                    │
     │ ✅ Dashboard showing judge statistics                                                                                                     │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ WEEK 5-8: Case Outcome Prediction Model                                                                                                   │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ Model Development:                                                                                                                        │
     │ # src/ml/outcome_prediction.py                                                                                                            │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ from xgboost import XGBClassifier                                                                                                         │
     │ from sklearn.model_selection import train_test_split                                                                                      │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ class OutcomePredictionModel:                                                                                                             │
     │     def __init__(self):                                                                                                                   │
     │         self.model = XGBClassifier(                                                                                                       │
     │             n_estimators=100,                                                                                                             │
     │             max_depth=8,                                                                                                                  │
     │             learning_rate=0.1                                                                                                             │
     │         )                                                                                                                                 │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │     def prepare_features(self, case):                                                                                                     │
     │         return {                                                                                                                          │
     │             # Case characteristics                                                                                                        │
     │             'case_type': self.encode_case_type(case['case_type']),                                                                        │
     │             'jurisdiction': self.encode_jurisdiction(case['jurisdiction']),                                                               │
     │             'case_complexity': self.calculate_complexity(case),                                                                           │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │             # Judge features                                                                                                              │
     │             'judge_plaintiff_win_rate': self.get_judge_win_rate(case['judge_id'], 'plaintiff'),                                           │
     │             'judge_reversal_rate': self.get_judge_reversal_rate(case['judge_id']),                                                        │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │             # Attorney features                                                                                                           │
     │             'plaintiff_attorney_win_rate': self.get_attorney_win_rate(case['plaintiff_attorney']),                                        │
     │             'defendant_attorney_win_rate': self.get_attorney_win_rate(case['defendant_attorney']),                                        │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │             # Case history features                                                                                                       │
     │             'motion_history': self.encode_motion_history(case),                                                                           │
     │             'discovery_disputes': case['discovery_disputes_count'],                                                                       │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │             # Precedent features                                                                                                          │
     │             'precedent_strength': self.calculate_precedent_strength(case),                                                                │
     │             'similar_case_outcomes': self.get_similar_case_stats(case)                                                                    │
     │         }                                                                                                                                 │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │     def train(self, training_data):                                                                                                       │
     │         X = [self.prepare_features(case) for case in training_data]                                                                       │
     │         y = [case['outcome'] for case in training_data]  # 0=defendant_win, 1=plaintiff_win, 2=settlement                                 │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │         X_train, X_test, y_train, y_test = train_test_split(X, y, test_size=0.2)                                                          │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │         self.model.fit(X_train, y_train)                                                                                                  │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │         accuracy = self.model.score(X_test, y_test)                                                                                       │
     │         print(f"Model accuracy: {accuracy}")  # Target: >75%                                                                              │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │     def predict(self, case):                                                                                                              │
     │         features = self.prepare_features(case)                                                                                            │
     │         probabilities = self.model.predict_proba([features])[0]                                                                           │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │         return {                                                                                                                          │
     │             'defendant_win_probability': probabilities[0],                                                                                │
     │             'plaintiff_win_probability': probabilities[1],                                                                                │
     │             'settlement_probability': probabilities[2],                                                                                   │
     │             'confidence': max(probabilities)                                                                                              │
     │         }                                                                                                                                 │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ Model Training:                                                                                                                           │
     │ - Collect 50,000 historical cases with known outcomes                                                                                     │
     │ - Train XGBoost model                                                                                                                     │
     │ - Achieve >75% accuracy target                                                                                                            │
     │ - Deploy model behind API                                                                                                                 │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ Deliverables:                                                                                                                             │
     │ ✅ Outcome prediction model trained (>75% accuracy)                                                                                       │
     │ ✅ API endpoint for predictions                                                                                                           │
     │ ✅ Model monitoring dashboard                                                                                                             │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ WEEK 9-12: Monitoring & Alerts System                                                                                                     │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ System Architecture:                                                                                                                      │
     │ # src/alerts/alert_system.py                                                                                                              │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ class LegalAlertSystem:                                                                                                                   │
     │     def __init__(self):                                                                                                                   │
     │         self.subscribers = {}                                                                                                             │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │     def subscribe(self, user_id, alert_type, filters):                                                                                    │
     │         """                                                                                                                               │
     │         Alert types:                                                                                                                      │
     │         - new_case_law                                                                                                                    │
     │         - statute_change                                                                                                                  │
     │         - adverse_citation                                                                                                                │
     │         - court_filing                                                                                                                    │
     │         - saved_search                                                                                                                    │
     │         """                                                                                                                               │
     │         alert = {                                                                                                                         │
     │             'user_id': user_id,                                                                                                           │
     │             'alert_type': alert_type,                                                                                                     │
     │             'filters': filters,                                                                                                           │
     │             'frequency': 'daily',  # or 'weekly', 'instant'                                                                               │
     │             'delivery': ['email', 'webhook']                                                                                              │
     │         }                                                                                                                                 │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │         self.store_subscription(alert)                                                                                                    │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │     def check_new_documents(self):                                                                                                        │
     │         """                                                                                                                               │
     │         Run daily job to check for matching documents                                                                                     │
     │         """                                                                                                                               │
     │         new_docs = self.get_documents_since_last_check()                                                                                  │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │         for doc in new_docs:                                                                                                              │
     │             matching_alerts = self.find_matching_subscriptions(doc)                                                                       │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │             for alert in matching_alerts:                                                                                                 │
     │                 self.send_notification(alert, doc)                                                                                        │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │     def check_adverse_citations(self):                                                                                                    │
     │         """                                                                                                                               │
     │         Check if user's saved cases have been distinguished/overruled                                                                     │
     │         """                                                                                                                               │
     │         for user_id in self.get_active_users():                                                                                           │
     │             saved_cases = self.get_user_saved_cases(user_id)                                                                              │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │             for case in saved_cases:                                                                                                      │
     │                 new_citations = self.get_new_citations(case['case_id'])                                                                   │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │                 adverse = [c for c in new_citations if c['treatment'] in ['DISTINGUISHED', 'OVERRULED', 'QUESTIONED']]                    │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │                 if adverse:                                                                                                               │
     │                     self.send_adverse_citation_alert(user_id, case, adverse)                                                              │
     │                                                                                                                                           │
     │ Notification Channels:                                                                                                                    │
     │ - Email (SendGrid)                                                                                                                        │
     │ - SMS (Twilio) - for urgent alerts                                                                                                        │
     │ - Webhooks (for your agentic AI system)                                                                                                   │
     │ - In-app notifications                                                                                                                    │

  - Islamic law coverage at 95% vs 99%+ for common law
  - Indigenous/tribal at 90% (sovereignty restrictions)
  - Some future/classified documents unavoidable

  2. Chunking Strategy: 92/100

  Strengths:
  - 65 chunk types vs industry standard 8-15
  - 7 specialized strategies (hierarchical, semantic, clause-based, procedural, financial, technical, hybrid)
  - Document-type-specific approaches
  - Smart overlap (0-150 tokens based on type)

  Gaps (-8 points):
  - No validation metrics for chunk quality
  - Missing chunk boundary detection for complex multi-lingual docs
  - No handling of OCR errors from scanned PDFs
  - Insufficient detail on table/image extraction from financial docs

  3. Technology Stack: 88/100

  Strengths:
  - Solid hybrid approach: Weaviate + Neo4j + BM25
  - BGE-M3 embeddings (multilingual, 1024-dim)
  - Reciprocal Rank Fusion for result merging
  - Managed services reduce ops burden

  Gaps (-12 points):
  - Critical: Cohere Rerank dependency (vendor lock-in, API costs scale with usage)
  - No fallback if Cohere pricing increases 10x
  - Missing self-hosted reranker migration timeline
  - Neo4j Aura Enterprise very expensive at scale ($15K+/month projected)
  - No cost optimization strategy beyond "migrate later"
  - Missing vector index optimization details (HNSW params, quantization)

  4. Retrieval Quality Targets: 85/100

  Strengths:
  - 97%+ precision@10 target
  - <500ms latency
  - Citation strength algorithm (KeyCite equivalent)
  - Cross-document synthesis

  Gaps (-15 points):
  - No baseline measurements - claiming 97% without current benchmark
  - Missing recall metrics (only precision specified)
  - No NDCG, MRR, or MAP metrics
  - No query-specific targets (statutory vs case law may differ)
  - Insufficient adversarial testing (edge cases, ambiguous queries)
  - No plan for continuous evaluation dataset

  5. Implementation Roadmap: 83/100

  Strengths:
  - 8 detailed phases over 25 months
  - Week-by-week breakdown
  - Clear milestones: MVP Month 7, Beta Month 13, Prod Month 25
  - Phased rollout by document complexity

  Gaps (-17 points):
  - Budget uncertainty: $1.56M → $2.24M (+43% increase)
  - Phase 0A too ambitious (4 weeks for team setup + infrastructure)
  - No buffer for integration delays with external data sources
  - Missing data acquisition timelines (Louisiana parishes, tribal courts)
  - Insufficient time for model fine-tuning (Legal-BERT NER)
  - No rollback plan if Phase 2-3 fail

  6. Data Sourcing Strategy: 78/100

  Strengths:
  - 3-tier access model (easy/moderate/difficult)
  - 512 types from free sources (51%)
  - Specific sources identified (BAILII, IndianKanoon, etc.)

  Gaps (-22 points):
  - Critical: 100 types (10%) marked "difficult access" with limited coverage
  - Tribal courts sovereignty issues unresolved
  - No backup for Louisiana parish data if blocked
  - Missing data refresh strategy (how often to re-scrape?)
  - No plan for paywalled content (LexisNexis exclusive docs)
  - OCR quality varies wildly for pre-2000 scanned docs
  - No handling of document versioning (point-in-time vs consolidated statutes)

  7. Metadata Schema: 90/100

  Strengths:
  - Universal fields + 35 type-specific extensions
  - Document lifecycle tracking (DRAFT/ENACTED/AMENDED/REPEALED)
  - Trust scores, verification status
  - Citation strength scoring

  Gaps (-10 points):
  - Missing author/drafter metadata for regulations
  - No confidence scores for OCR'd text
  - Insufficient multilingual metadata (treaty translations)
  - No versioning for amended documents

  8. Graph Schema (Neo4j): 84/100

  Strengths:
  - 54 node types, 70 relationship types
  - Rich citation network (CITES, OVERRULES, FOLLOWS, DISTINGUISHES)
  - Cross-document relationships (IMPLEMENTS, INTERPRETS, AMENDS)

  Gaps (-16 points):
  - Missing temporal relationships (SUPERSEDES_AS_OF date)
  - No weighted relationships (how strong is citation?)
  - Insufficient reverse lookups (all cases citing Section X)
  - Missing graph algorithms (PageRank for case importance)
  - No plan for graph analytics at scale (10M+ nodes)

  9. API Design: 86/100

  Strengths:
  - RESTful FastAPI design
  - Clear integration with agentic AI
  - Retrieval-only focus (generation handled externally)

  Gaps (-14 points):
  - Missing rate limiting strategy
  - No API versioning plan
  - Insufficient auth/authorization details
  - Missing SLA guarantees for uptime
  - No webhook support for real-time updates

  10. Competitive Position: 91/100

  Strengths:
  - Claims #1 position vs LexisNexis (850 types), Westlaw (800 types)
  - 15-20% more document types than competitors
  - Only system with 2024 compliance docs
  - Unique jurisdictions (Scottish, Louisiana, tribal)

  Gaps (-9 points):
  - Unproven claims - competitors may have unlisted document types
  - Missing feature parity analysis (Westlaw has 120+ features beyond retrieval)
  - No plan for competitor response (what if LexisNexis adds 200 types?)
  - Insufficient moat - taxonomy can be copied
